239|a4a35b|    private func getTreeSitterLanguage(for filename: String) -> Runestone.TreeSitterLanguage? {
240|98942b|        let ext = (filename as NSString).pathExtension.lowercased()
241|82335e|        let lastComponent = (filename as NSString).lastPathComponent.lowercased()
242|d6ed84|        
243|ab25ec|        // Special-case filenames without extensions
244|013551|        if lastComponent == "dockerfile" || lastComponent.hasPrefix("dockerfile.") {
245|274790|            return nil // Bash support not in package list yet
246|5f3077|        }
247|bf07fd|        if lastComponent == ".env" || lastComponent.hasPrefix(".env.") {
248|3e3e36|            return nil // Plain text
249|5f3077|        }
250|828d40|        if lastComponent == "makefile" || lastComponent == "gnumakefile" {
251|274790|            return nil // Bash support not in package list yet
252|5f3077|        }

255|5f3077|        }

257|4d9419|            return TreeSitterLanguage.json

259|d6ed84|

309|b4687f|    
310|6a2db5|    private func countLines(in text: String) -> Int {
311|ee3501|        guard !text.isEmpty else { return 1 }
312|c746a1|        var count = 1
313|48817a|        var index = text.startIndex
314|42136d|        while index < text.endIndex {
315|4396fc|            if text[index] == "\n" {
316|31d0c1|                count += 1
317|a7dc16|            }
318|3a0fcb|            index = text.index(after: index)
319|5f3077|        }
320|c7b6e6|        return count
321|27e597|    }

360|bc1cc6|            textSyncWorkItem?.cancel()
361|3070d1|

364|150252|                guard let self = self else { return }
365|84d674|                self.isUpdatingFromTextView = true
366|0ae33b|                defer { self.isUpdatingFromTextView = false }

374|4e2d32|                }
375|a7dc16|            }

377|eaaa24|            // Schedule the update after debounce interval
378|587c05|            textSyncWorkItem = workItem
379|c3b6ab|            DispatchQueue.main.asyncAfter(deadline: .now() + debounceInterval, execute: workItem)
380|5f3077|        }

432|638123|        private func updateCursorPosition(in textView: TextView) {
433|e844dd|            let selectedRange = textView.selectedRange
434|0c3128|            let text = textView.text as NSString
435|c0763f|            let cursorLocation = selectedRange.location
436|3070d1|            
437|3c0f5f|            // Calculate line and column from cursor location
438|2bf772|            var lineNumber = 1
439|b2dc74|            var columnNumber = 1
440|895788|            var currentLineStart = 0
441|3070d1|            
442|30ee03|            for i in 0..<min(cursorLocation, text.length) {
443|76817f|                if text.character(at: i) == UInt16(UnicodeScalar("\n").value) {
444|4ae0f3|                    lineNumber += 1
445|1230ab|                    currentLineStart = i + 1
446|4e2d32|                }
447|a7dc16|            }
448|3070d1|            
449|fe9f83|            // Column is the offset from the start of the current line
450|2ea6e9|            columnNumber = cursorLocation - currentLineStart + 1
451|3070d1|            
452|13f4e9|            // Update bindings on main thread to avoid SwiftUI state update warnings
453|ebb427|            DispatchQueue.main.async {
454|62efc4|                self.parent.cursorIndex = cursorLocation
455|29327f|                self.parent.currentLineNumber = lineNumber
456|975d29|                self.parent.currentColumn = columnNumber
457|a7dc16|            }
458|5f3077|        }

589|ff2c29|    // MARK: - Syntax Highlighting
590|b4687f|    
591|77216f|    func textColor(for rawHighlightName: String) -> UIColor? {
592|364fdf|        // Map TreeSitter highlight names to colors
593|077102|        // See: https://tree-sitter.github.io/tree-sitter/syntax-highlighting#highlights
594|a3c6a6|        let highlightName = rawHighlightName.lowercased()
595|d6ed84|        
596|3e8301|        // Debug: Log ALL highlight names to console (ENABLED FOR DEBUGGING)
597|1aa7f0|        print("🎨 HIGHLIGHT: '\(rawHighlightName)' -> ", terminator: "")
598|d6ed84|        
599|5f2431|        // Keywords
600|347daa|        if highlightName.contains("keyword") {
601|e0cdb7|            print("keyword (blue)")
602|11656d|            return _keywordColor
603|5f3077|        }
604|d6ed84|        
605|c13ace|        // JSON/Object keys - MUST return color for specific patterns
606|164d0a|        // TreeSitter JSON emits BOTH "string.special.key" AND "string" for keys
607|63f969|        // We handle specific patterns first, then skip generic "string" to avoid overwrite
608|929452|        if highlightName.hasPrefix("string.special") ||
609|7d9926|           highlightName.contains("label") ||
610|81c371|           highlightName.contains("property.definition") {
611|7612b6|            print("key/label (light blue)")
612|5086b7|            return _variableColor  // Light blue #9CDCFE for keys
613|5f3077|        }
614|d6ed84|        
615|5fe933|        // Strings - but NOT if it's JUST "string" (let specific matches win)
616|dcb001|        // Only color strings that are clearly values, not potential keys
617|ab3d14|        if highlightName.contains("string") {
618|5655ac|            print("string (orange)")
619|f09755|            return _stringColor  // Orange #CE9178 for string values
620|5f3077|        }
621|d6ed84|        
622|f425cd|        // Numbers and constants
623|a2036f|        if highlightName.contains("number") || highlightName == "constant.numeric" {
624|57bea5|            print("number (green)")
625|da9aee|            return _numberColor
626|5f3077|        }
627|d6ed84|        
628|185d89|        // Comments
629|f4b237|        if highlightName.contains("comment") {
630|e46058|            return _commentColor
631|5f3077|        }
632|d6ed84|        
633|4d76db|        // Functions and methods
634|915dec|        if highlightName.contains("function") || highlightName.contains("method") {
635|69dae5|            return _functionColor
636|5f3077|        }
637|d6ed84|        
638|5853d5|        // Types, classes, structs
639|a68e63|        if highlightName.contains("type") || highlightName.contains("class") ||
640|fe7d45|           highlightName.contains("struct") || highlightName.contains("interface") ||
641|7850d5|           highlightName.contains("enum") {
642|079364|            return _typeColor
643|5f3077|        }
644|d6ed84|        
645|100acb|        // Variables, parameters, properties
646|87a47d|        if highlightName.contains("variable") || highlightName.contains("parameter") ||
647|6198a9|           highlightName.contains("property") || highlightName.contains("field") {
648|0e23b9|            return _variableColor
649|5f3077|        }
650|d6ed84|        
651|f1a54a|        // Constants and booleans - use keyword color
652|cc358f|        if highlightName.contains("constant") || highlightName.contains("boolean") {
653|11656d|            return _keywordColor
654|5f3077|        }
655|d6ed84|        
656|b158fb|        // Operators - use keyword color
657|1a986d|        if highlightName.contains("operator") {
658|11656d|            return _keywordColor
659|5f3077|        }
660|d6ed84|        
661|8737fd|        // Namespaces and modules - use type color
662|d04ebe|        if highlightName.contains("namespace") || highlightName.contains("module") {
663|079364|            return _typeColor
664|5f3077|        }
665|d6ed84|        
666|d204ef|        // Tags (HTML, XML) - use type color
667|e21ab6|        if highlightName.contains("tag") {
668|079364|            return _typeColor
669|5f3077|        }
670|d6ed84|        
671|2abb6b|        // Attributes - use variable color
672|91f255|        if highlightName.contains("attribute") {
673|0e23b9|            return _variableColor
674|5f3077|        }
675|d6ed84|        
676|bb1e1f|        // Spell checking highlights - ignore (return nil to use default)
677|1dc697|        if highlightName.contains("spell") {
678|1c8557|            return nil
679|5f3077|        }
680|d6ed84|        
681|3d22f9|        // Include/import statements - use keyword color
682|fd8f58|        if highlightName.contains("include") {
683|11656d|            return _keywordColor
684|5f3077|        }
685|d6ed84|        
686|c1e1a1|        // Default: use standard text color
687|e35567|        print("nil (default)")
688|c2ae65|        return nil
689|27e597|    }
690|b4687f|    
691|666dc2|    func fontTraits(for rawHighlightName: String) -> FontTraits {
692|a3c6a6|        let highlightName = rawHighlightName.lowercased()
693|d6ed84|        
694|f6d691|        // Make comments italic
695|f4b237|        if highlightName.contains("comment") {
696|9ac334|            return .italic
697|5f3077|        }
698|d6ed84|        
699|556e36|        // Make keywords bold
700|347daa|        if highlightName.contains("keyword") {
701|7775b3|            return .bold
702|5f3077|        }
703|d6ed84|        
704|b72a10|        return []
705|27e597|    }

800|adc83b|
801|b096af|            // NOTE: We intentionally do NOT manipulate undoManager.disableUndoRegistration/enableUndoRegistration
802|bf1d61|            // here. UITextView's internal undo manager state machine is fragile and can crash with
803|b755b7|            // "enableUndoRegistration may only be invoked with matching call to disableUndoRegistration"
804|dd5c2c|            // when attributedText assignment triggers internal undo callbacks.
805|75d880|            // 
806|ff6bb4|            // Instead, we let the system handle undo naturally. The trade-off is that syntax highlighting
807|92400f|            // changes might add noise to the undo stack, but this is preferable to crashing.
808|3070d1|

811|adc83b|

1079|a5bb65|            let selection = textView.selectedRange
1080|b3d375|            let text = textView.text ?? ""
1081|3070d1|            
1082|e88a70|            // Only highlight when there's a selection (word selected)
1083|e3e49b|            guard selection.length > 0 else { return }
1084|3070d1|            
1085|4d2541|            // Get occurrences
1086|b477a5|            let occurrences = WordOccurrenceHighlighter.shared.findOccurrences(in: text, selection: selection)
1087|3070d1|            
1088|c2b3b8|            // Need at least 2 occurrences (including the selected one) to show highlights
1089|b28715|            guard occurrences.count >= 2 else { return }
1090|3070d1|            
1091|6035ba|            let theme = ThemeManager.shared.currentTheme
1092|1cf7af|            let highlightColor = WordOccurrenceHighlighter.highlightColor(for: theme)
1093|3070d1|            
1094|bf8605|            // Apply highlights to all occurrences EXCEPT the current selection
1095|f25c3b|            for occurrence in occurrences {
1096|509884|                // Skip the currently selected occurrence
1097|2e9f1b|                if occurrence.range.location == selection.location && occurrence.range.length == selection.length {
1098|f41bef|                    continue

1110|d694db|/// TextKit layout manager that collapses line fragments for lines marked folded in CodeFoldingManager.
1111|a841a1|/// This is a view-level folding implementation (it does NOT modify the underlying text).
1112|bc1fac|final class FoldingLayoutManager: NSLayoutManager, NSLayoutManagerDelegate {
1113|41027e|    weak var ownerTextView: EditorTextView?
1114|adc83b|
1115|b3c6ad|    override init() {
1116|15cfe8|        super.init()
1117|95d040|        self.delegate = self
1118|27e597|    }
1119|adc83b|

1123|27e597|    }
1124|adc83b|
1125|efe359|    func layoutManager(
1126|809adb|        _ layoutManager: NSLayoutManager,
1127|1c55e7|        shouldSetLineFragmentRect lineFragmentRect: UnsafeMutablePointer<CGRect>,
1128|98c806|        lineFragmentUsedRect: UnsafeMutablePointer<CGRect>,
1129|bc48e6|        baselineOffset: UnsafeMutablePointer<CGFloat>,
1130|fcdc4d|        in textContainer: NSTextContainer,
1131|1874c5|        forGlyphRange glyphRange: NSRange
1132|54d8bb|    ) -> Bool {
1133|04c681|        guard let owner = ownerTextView,
1134|059837|              let foldingManager = owner.foldingManager,
1135|e73db4|              let fileId = owner.fileId
1136|4ebc7a|        else {
1137|e2e187|            return false
1138|5f3077|        }
1139|adc83b|
1140|9de2dc|        // Convert glyphRange -> characterRange so we can compute the line index.
1141|9471e8|        let charRange = self.characterRange(forGlyphRange: glyphRange, actualGlyphRange: nil)
1142|e786e2|        let loc = max(0, charRange.location)
1143|adc83b|
1144|b1964a|        let full = (self.textStorage?.string ?? "") as NSString
1145|ca159a|        let lineIndex = FoldingLayoutManager.lineIndex(atUTF16Location: loc, in: full)
1146|adc83b|
1147|7b763c|        if foldingManager.isLineFolded(fileId: fileId, line: lineIndex) {
1148|2e29aa|            // Collapse this visual line fragment.
1149|52dd91|            lineFragmentRect.pointee.size.height = 0
1150|3edd23|            lineFragmentUsedRect.pointee.size.height = 0
1151|eaeafe|            baselineOffset.pointee = 0
1152|40cfc4|            return true
1153|5f3077|        }
1154|adc83b|
1155|dc1500|        return false
1156|27e597|    }
1157|adc83b|
1158|8aab29|    private static func lineIndex(atUTF16Location loc: Int, in text: NSString) -> Int {
1159|470ca2|        if loc <= 0 { return 0 }
1160|adc83b|
1161|cdd09d|        let capped = min(loc, text.length)
1162|d609cf|        var line = 0
1163|d0a79c|        var searchStart = 0
1164|adc83b|
1165|bbb957|        while searchStart < capped {
1166|fc657a|            let r = text.range(of: "\n", options: [], range: NSRange(location: searchStart, length: capped - searchStart))
1167|d8b23a|            if r.location == NSNotFound { break }
1168|e2b919|            line += 1
1169|dae32a|            let next = r.location + 1
1170|af699d|            if next >= capped { break }
1171|317174|            searchStart = next
1172|5f3077|        }
1173|adc83b|
1174|bf9a21|        return line
1175|27e597|    }

1698|114d31|    private func highlight(_ text: String, language: SyntaxLanguage) -> NSAttributedString {
1699|04be19|        let attributed = NSMutableAttributedString(string: text)
1700|576a7a|        let fullRange = NSRange(location: 0, length: text.utf16.count)
1701|d6ed84|

1703|b792d5|        let baseFont = UIFont.monospacedSystemFont(ofSize: baseFontSize, weight: .regular)

1705|8f20b4|        attributed.addAttribute(.foregroundColor, value: UIColor(theme.editorForeground), range: fullRange)
1706|d6ed84|

1708|f3155b|        switch language {

1710|66c2b6|        case .javascript, .jsx: highlightJavaScript(attributed, text: text, isTS: false)
1711|f878d3|        case .typescript, .tsx: highlightJavaScript(attributed, text: text, isTS: true)
1712|bf5ad7|        case .python: highlightPython(attributed, text: text)
1713|694371|        case .html, .xml: highlightHTML(attributed, text: text)
1714|d59b9e|        case .css, .scss, .less: highlightCSS(attributed, text: text)
1715|fef33c|        case .json: highlightJSON(attributed, text: text)
1716|d045a0|        case .markdown: highlightMarkdown(attributed, text: text)
1717|3d7ac9|        case .rust: highlightRust(attributed, text: text)
1718|22c786|        case .go: highlightGo(attributed, text: text)
1719|aa1226|        case .java, .kotlin: highlightJava(attributed, text: text)

1721|15fa67|        case .ruby: highlightRuby(attributed, text: text)
1722|b2c03c|        case .php: highlightPHP(attributed, text: text)

1736|43cc7c|    // MARK: - Bracket Pair Colorization
1737|b4687f|    
1738|6375f9|    private func highlightBracketPairs(_ attributed: NSMutableAttributedString, text: String) {
1739|15e10d|        let brackets: [Character] = ["{", "}", "[", "]", "(", ")"]
1740|d14333|        let pairs: [Character: Character] = ["}": "{", "]": "[", ")": "("]
1741|d6ed84|        
1742|99a4a9|        var stack: [(char: Character, index: Int, depth: Int)] = []
1743|6e4cea|        let colors = [
1744|20317f|            UIColor(theme.bracketPair1),
1745|5f8621|            UIColor(theme.bracketPair2),
1746|4c6756|            UIColor(theme.bracketPair3),
1747|5eabae|            UIColor(theme.bracketPair4),
1748|f54b47|            UIColor(theme.bracketPair5),
1749|930dd3|            UIColor(theme.bracketPair6)
1750|220505|        ]
1751|d6ed84|        
1752|44166e|        // Scan text for brackets
1753|439013|        // Note: In a real implementation, we should skip brackets inside strings/comments
1754|2bdb67|        // But since we apply this LAST, we can try to respect existing string/comment colors
1755|f89202|        // OR implement a more robust parser. For now, simple scan.
1756|d6ed84|        
1757|8945b5|        // Optimization: Use scanner or direct iteration
1758|4fc7f4|        let nsString = text as NSString
1759|9203e3|        var index = 0
1760|d6ed84|        
1761|810ca8|        while index < text.utf16.count {
1762|4f9ad4|            let char = nsString.character(at: index)
1763|7e8ad3|            if let scalar = UnicodeScalar(char) {
1764|e4a370|                let c = Character(scalar)
1765|216278|                
1766|cbd2a8|                if brackets.contains(c) {
1767|1b3670|                    // Check if it's already colored as string/comment (heuristic)
1768|149e03|                    // If color is string/comment, skip
1769|850f04|                    // (Requires iterating attributes, which is slow. We'll just apply on top for now)
1770|dd2193|                    
1771|996925|                    if let open = pairs[c] { // Closing bracket
1772|6114f3|                        if let last = stack.last, last.char == open {
1773|1469ee|                            // Match found
1774|28d302|                            let depth = last.depth
1775|4ca6c1|                            let color = colors[depth % colors.count]
1776|e4abf2|                            
1777|c40423|                            attributed.addAttribute(.foregroundColor, value: color, range: NSRange(location: index, length: 1))
1778|9f0f64|                            attributed.addAttribute(.foregroundColor, value: color, range: NSRange(location: last.index, length: 1))
1779|e4abf2|                            
1780|fd0ca5|                            stack.removeLast()
1781|65e2f4|                        } else {
1782|79dbca|                            // Mismatched or extra closing bracket - unexpected
1783|b93d0a|                            // Keep default color or mark red? Default for now.
1784|392b35|                        }
1785|3a0c6a|                    } else { // Opening bracket
1786|0232e2|                        let depth = stack.count
1787|802404|                        stack.append((c, index, depth))
1788|956cfe|                        
1789|6eedf4|                        // We'll color it when (and if) we find the match, or here?
1790|74f3b7|                        // Better to color here tentatively, but matching is better.
1791|66092b|                        // Let's color tentatively based on depth.
1792|f150d9|                        let color = colors[depth % colors.count]
1793|65df06|                        attributed.addAttribute(.foregroundColor, value: color, range: NSRange(location: index, length: 1))
1794|c9717a|                    }
1795|4e2d32|                }
1796|a7dc16|            }
1797|fe2650|            index += 1
1798|5f3077|        }
1799|27e597|    }

260|4e4994|    private func executeSearch() -> [SearchResult] {
261|808213|        guard let core = editorCore else { return [] }
262|06469e|        guard let regex = buildRegex() else { return [] }
263|adc83b|
264|b128e6|        struct Target {
265|d0d64f|            let url: URL?
266|649854|            let filePath: String
267|062bcc|            let fileName: String
268|6ffdc2|            let content: String
269|5f3077|        }
270|adc83b|
271|422382|        let targets: [Target] = {
272|450a38|            switch searchScope {
273|08df20|            case .currentFile:
274|c935e6|                guard let tab = core.activeTab else { return [] }
275|666545|                let path = tab.url?.path ?? tab.fileName
276|57a63d|                return [Target(url: tab.url, filePath: path, fileName: tab.fileName, content: tab.content)]
277|adc83b|
278|231fff|            case .openFiles:
279|09a4e8|                return core.tabs.map { tab in
280|66779a|                    let path = tab.url?.path ?? tab.fileName
281|be9fba|                    return Target(url: tab.url, filePath: path, fileName: tab.fileName, content: tab.content)
282|4e2d32|                }
283|adc83b|
284|2fb721|            case .workspace:
285|481d56|                guard let tree = core.fileNavigator?.fileTree else { return [] }
286|3d2cac|                let urls = collectFileURLs(from: tree)
287|c4e083|                return urls.compactMap { url in
288|e86233|                    guard let content = try? String(contentsOf: url, encoding: .utf8) else { return nil }
289|3223da|                    return Target(url: url, filePath: url.path, fileName: url.lastPathComponent, content: content)
290|4e2d32|                }
291|a7dc16|            }
292|41cc2d|        }()
293|adc83b|
294|ede8fe|        var results: [SearchResult] = []
295|87d422|        results.reserveCapacity(64)
296|adc83b|
297|7e02cf|        for target in targets {
298|e64b6f|            let text = target.content
299|922eef|            let nsText = text as NSString
300|adc83b|
301|a53603|            let searchRange: NSRange
302|c50c1e|            if searchInSelection,
303|e6cc02|               searchScope == .currentFile,
304|9b8ef5|               let selection = core.currentSelectionRange {
305|92f918|                searchRange = selection
306|f5a6eb|            } else {
307|fd803f|                searchRange = NSRange(location: 0, length: nsText.length)
308|a7dc16|            }
309|adc83b|
310|5842db|            let matches = regex.matches(in: text, options: [], range: searchRange)
311|7c58fe|            for match in matches {
312|ed8ef0|                let r = match.range
313|30dcc2|                guard let swiftRange = Range(r, in: text) else { continue }
314|adc83b|
315|9f4e6b|                // 1-based line number
316|854f7d|                let prefix = nsText.substring(to: min(r.location, nsText.length))
317|caf675|                let lineNumber = prefix.components(separatedBy: "\n").count
318|adc83b|
319|7f7e0b|                // Full line content
320|bab0af|                let lineRange = nsText.lineRange(for: r)
321|b88e01|                var lineContent = nsText.substring(with: lineRange)
322|0bfc40|                lineContent = lineContent.trimmingCharacters(in: .newlines)
323|adc83b|
324|944744|                results.append(
325|5c7081|                    SearchResult(
326|d50448|                        filePath: target.filePath,
327|ab39a1|                        fileName: target.fileName,
328|36535d|                        url: target.url,
329|3d467c|                        lineNumber: lineNumber,
330|e9c207|                        lineContent: lineContent,
331|817f47|                        matchRange: swiftRange,
332|bd73c0|                        matchNSRange: r,
333|c65676|                        contextBefore: nil,
334|9ce3a8|                        contextAfter: nil
335|1961a4|                    )
336|6f642e|                )

338|5f3077|        }
339|adc83b|

341|27e597|    }

343|49f5dd|    private func buildRegex() -> NSRegularExpression? {
344|aa8b8c|        guard !searchQuery.isEmpty else { return nil }
345|adc83b|
346|d13bab|        let pattern: String
347|2c0ffc|        if useRegex {
348|ee8ad7|            pattern = searchQuery

355|adc83b|

357|27e597|    }

693|5d97cf|        switch lineNumbersStyle {
694|a6eb36|        case "relative":
695|b0622f|            let lineNumber = lineIndex + 1

698|5040ac|        case "interval":
699|b0622f|            let lineNumber = lineIndex + 1
700|bc3fe3|            return (lineNumber == 1 || lineNumber % 5 == 0) ? "\(lineNumber)" : ""

7|703558|## Vision
8|adc83b|
9|57cd9f|A **native Swift/SwiftUI** code editor that brings the full VSCode experience to iPadOS:
10|adc83b|
11|458185|- 📝 Full-featured code editor with syntax highlighting
12|d3aad5|- 🧠 Language Server Protocol (LSP) for autocomplete, errors, go-to-definition
13|fd439a|- 🔌 Extension system (compatible with VSCode extensions where possible)
14|ee3989|- 📁 File system: iCloud Drive, local files, SSH/SFTP, GitHub
15|2342de|- 🖥️ Integrated terminal emulator
16|cc7976|- 🌳 Git integration (stage, commit, push, pull, branches)
17|46a1b4|- ⌨️ Full keyboard shortcut support
18|a940f2|- 📱 iPad-native: Split View, Slide Over, Stage Manager
19|cf3e0c|- 🎨 Themes (dark/light, custom)
20|212231|- 🔍 Global search, find & replace with regex
21|adc83b|

23|adc83b|
24|1a0775|```
25|047ff8|┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐

220|7dcb1c|    func updateUIView(_ textView: UITextView, context: Context) {
221|855109|        // CRITICAL: Update coordinator's parent reference to current struct
222|333ede|        // SwiftUI creates new struct instances on each update, so this keeps
223|620e32|        // coordinator in sync with current bindings and properties
224|aa6fd6|        context.coordinator.parent = self
225|d6ed84|        
226|0a58ec|        // CRITICAL FIX: Apply initial highlighting FIRST on the very first updateUIView call
227|211a1a|        // This fixes the bug where syntax highlighting only appears after typing.
228|815fc1|        // makeUIView applies it, but the view may not be fully in hierarchy yet,
229|ab2ed7|        // causing the attributed text to be lost. This ensures it's applied reliably.
230|d721d6|        if !context.coordinator.hasAppliedInitialHighlighting && !textView.text.isEmpty {
231|140558|            context.coordinator.applySyntaxHighlighting(to: textView)
232|4dd2eb|            context.coordinator.hasAppliedInitialHighlighting = true
233|5f3077|        }
234|d6ed84|        
235|31e4e9|        // Update colors when theme changes
236|5ee36b|        // NOTE: Only set backgroundColor and tintColor here. Do NOT set textColor
237|d2a31c|        // as it interferes with attributedText syntax highlighting colors.
238|2ba8b3|        // The foreground color is handled entirely by the attributedText.
239|e5b95a|        textView.backgroundColor = UIColor(ThemeManager.shared.currentTheme.editorBackground)
240|0c4521|        textView.tintColor = UIColor(ThemeManager.shared.currentTheme.cursor)
241|d6ed84|        
242|330f1a|        if let editorView = textView as? EditorTextView {
243|397219|            editorView.updateThemeColors(theme: ThemeManager.shared.currentTheme)
244|5f3077|        }
245|d6ed84|        
246|c506e2|        // Update font size if changed (using explicit fontSize parameter for proper SwiftUI updates)
247|1e3b94|        if let currentFont = textView.font, currentFont.pointSize != fontSize {
248|e844dd|            let selectedRange = textView.selectedRange
249|441e85|            textView.font = UIFont.monospacedSystemFont(ofSize: fontSize, weight: .regular)
250|140558|            context.coordinator.applySyntaxHighlighting(to: textView)
251|335b1a|            textView.selectedRange = selectedRange
252|3070d1|            
253|53ed35|            // Update line height
254|f4daab|            if let font = textView.font {
255|f143b8|                DispatchQueue.main.async {
256|6dfb70|                    self.lineHeight = font.lineHeight
257|4e2d32|                }
258|a7dc16|            }
259|5f3077|        }
260|d6ed84|        
261|d764b8|        // Update text if changed externally
262|c4b3de|        if textView.text != text {
263|e844dd|            let selectedRange = textView.selectedRange
264|bf1757|            textView.text = text
265|140558|            context.coordinator.applySyntaxHighlighting(to: textView)

72|8aab29|    private static func lineIndex(atUTF16Location loc: Int, in text: NSString) -> Int {
73|470ca2|        if loc <= 0 { return 0 }
74|adc83b|
75|cdd09d|        let capped = min(loc, text.length)
76|d609cf|        var line = 0
77|d0a79c|        var searchStart = 0
78|adc83b|
79|bbb957|        while searchStart < capped {
80|fc657a|            let r = text.range(of: "\n", options: [], range: NSRange(location: searchStart, length: capped - searchStart))
81|d8b23a|            if r.location == NSNotFound { break }

83|dae32a|            let next = r.location + 1
84|af699d|            if next >= capped { break }
85|317174|            searchStart = next
86|5f3077|        }
87|adc83b|
88|bf9a21|        return line
89|27e597|    }

138|c2e8b0|        let prefixLower = context.prefix.lowercased()

87|ff38bb|    func findAllBracketPairs(in text: String) -> [BracketPair] {
88|dcb8ea|        var pairs: [BracketPair] = []
89|3e3195|        var stacks: [BracketType: [Int]] = [:]
90|d6ed84|        
91|f022b0|        for type in BracketType.allCases {
92|54a3ff|            stacks[type] = []
93|5f3077|        }
94|d6ed84|        
95|9df2e8|        let chars = Array(text)
96|e79b86|        var inString = false
97|11024e|        var stringChar: Character = "\""
98|e550d2|        var escapeNext = false
99|d6ed84|        
100|f0ad7e|        for (index, char) in chars.enumerated() {
101|11cf75|            // Handle escape sequences
102|5c254a|            if escapeNext {
103|b7c801|                escapeNext = false
104|1df510|                continue
105|a7dc16|            }

108|78ee7a|                escapeNext = true

113|631cb5|            if char == "\"" || char == "'" {

118|dffb64|                    inString = false
119|4e2d32|                }
120|1df510|                continue

122|3070d1|            
123|801179|            // Skip brackets inside strings
124|28e059|            if inString { continue }
125|3070d1|

139|27e597|    }

234|d6ed84|

236|fe2046|        // We'll do a basic scan that handles most common cases
237|267cd6|        for i in stride(from: startIndex - 1, through: 0, by: -1) {

248|1df510|                continue

256|ae2b9f|                depth -= 1

258|125c3c|                    return i

95|d6ed84|

99|c5b1d1|        var regionStack: [(startLine: Int, label: String)] = []
100|adc83b|
101|ff8cec|        // If we detect a declaration/function/control-flow whose opening brace is on a later line,
102|724e06|        // we mark that brace line so it won't be treated as a standalone generic block.
103|945b20|        var braceLinesClaimed: Set<Int> = []
104|adc83b|
105|cce061|        // Used to prevent duplicate regions for grouped constructs (imports, // comments)
106|0cdafa|        var previousNonEmptyWasImport = false

108|d6ed84|        
109|035521|        for (index, line) in lines.enumerated() {

111|8a2732|            let leadingWhitespace = line.prefix { $0 == " " || $0 == "\t" }.count
112|3070d1|            
113|4be2b3|            // Skip empty lines for most detections
114|94f56f|            guard !trimmed.isEmpty else { continue }
115|adc83b|
116|096595|            // MARK: - Close blocks BEFORE opening new ones (handles "} else {" correctly)
117|3c0070|            if trimmed.hasPrefix("}") {
118|f8c18c|                // Count consecutive leading '}' so we can pop multiple blocks for lines like "}}"
119|7f8903|                let closeCount = max(1, trimmed.prefix { $0 == "}" }.count)
120|539d99|                for _ in 0..<closeCount {
121|75d4ef|                    if let lastBlock = blockStack.popLast() {
122|23d31e|                        if index - lastBlock.startLine > 1 {
123|9008b5|                            regions.append(FoldRegion(

125|419111|                                endLine: index,

127|b802b0|                                label: lastBlock.label
128|b6c95b|                            ))
129|392b35|                        }
130|c9717a|                    }
131|4e2d32|                }
132|a7dc16|            }
133|3070d1|            
134|454897|            // MARK: - Region Detection (#region, #pragma mark, MARK:)
135|18ca54|            if let label = detectRegionStart(trimmed) {
136|77dbe9|                regionStack.append((index, label))
137|a9d0ef|            } else if detectRegionEnd(trimmed) {
138|24137d|                if let region = regionStack.popLast() {
139|58d5c1|                    if index - region.startLine > 1 {
140|22c663|                        regions.append(FoldRegion(

142|46d058|                            endLine: index,

149|3070d1|            
150|b80509|            // MARK: - Import Statement Detection (group consecutive imports once)
151|25e1cc|            if trimmed.hasPrefix("import ") {

187|0b3758|                previousNonEmptyWasSingleLineComment = false

203|fc4e2f|    func updateRatio(at index: Int, delta: CGFloat, totalSize: CGFloat) {
204|aa52a4|        guard index < splitRatios.count - 1 else { return }
205|d6ed84|        
206|f7ce87|        let deltaRatio = delta / totalSize
207|019df3|        let minRatio: CGFloat = 0.15
208|d6ed84|        
209|3f9e36|        let newRatio1 = splitRatios[index] + deltaRatio
210|d4621b|        let newRatio2 = splitRatios[index + 1] - deltaRatio
211|d6ed84|        
212|289da5|        if newRatio1 >= minRatio && newRatio2 >= minRatio {
213|6df122|            splitRatios[index] = newRatio1
214|7b2474|            splitRatios[index + 1] = newRatio2
215|5f3077|        }
216|27e597|    }

705|46d3db|    private func displayText(for lineIndex: Int) -> String {
706|5d97cf|        switch lineNumbersStyle {
707|a6eb36|        case "relative":
708|b0622f|            let lineNumber = lineIndex + 1
709|44bb33|            if lineNumber == currentLine { return "\(lineNumber)" }
710|5e67df|            return "\(abs(lineNumber - currentLine))"
711|adc83b|
712|5040ac|        case "interval":
713|b0622f|            let lineNumber = lineIndex + 1
714|bc3fe3|            return (lineNumber == 1 || lineNumber % 5 == 0) ? "\(lineNumber)" : ""
715|adc83b|
716|520b7d|        default:
717|3880c0|            return "\(lineIndex + 1)"
718|5f3077|        }
719|27e597|    }

1009|844dfd|            let closeToOpen: [unichar: unichar] = [125: 123, 41: 40, 93: 91] // } -> {, ) -> (, ] -> [

147|f96259|    /// Returns the filtered, sorted, and limited results
148|f32b09|    var processedResults: [FileSearchResult] {
149|1a5bc0|        var filtered = rawResults
150|d6ed84|        
151|0a214d|        // 1. Filter by binary files
152|99c850|        if excludeBinaryFiles {
153|9b3c53|            filtered = filtered.filter { result in
154|74a475|                let ext = (result.fileName as NSString).pathExtension.lowercased()
155|979d9d|                return !binaryExtensions.contains(where: { $0.lowercased().hasSuffix(ext) })
156|a7dc16|            }
157|5f3077|        }
158|d6ed84|        
159|23706c|        // 2. Filter by selected extensions
160|8f0448|        if !selectedExtensions.isEmpty {
161|9b3c53|            filtered = filtered.filter { result in
162|74a475|                let ext = (result.fileName as NSString).pathExtension.lowercased()
163|db0fb9|                return selectedExtensions.contains { $0.lowercased().dropFirst() == ext }
164|a7dc16|            }
165|5f3077|        }
166|d6ed84|        
167|e35546|        // 3. Sort results
168|b5c3d5|        filtered = filtered.sorted { lhs, rhs in
169|cc07ab|            switch sortOption {
170|2eb58c|            case .fileName:
171|c61e48|                return sortAscending ? lhs.fileName < rhs.fileName : lhs.fileName > rhs.fileName
172|7a14db|            case .path:
173|8db7c1|                return sortAscending ? lhs.path < rhs.path : lhs.path > rhs.path
174|f24236|            case .matches:
175|beb3b2|                return sortAscending ? lhs.matches.count < rhs.matches.count : lhs.matches.count > rhs.matches.count
176|a7dc16|            }
177|5f3077|        }
178|d6ed84|        
179|b622d3|        // 4. Apply result limit
180|2f53d7|        if let maxCount = resultLimit.maxCount, filtered.count > maxCount {
181|78a06d|            filtered = Array(filtered.prefix(maxCount))
182|5f3077|        }
183|d6ed84|        
184|ed0d9a|        return filtered
185|27e597|    }
186|b4687f|    
187|afa680|    /// Group results by directory if enabled
188|bf562e|    var groupedResults: [(key: String, results: [FileSearchResult])] {
189|cfef88|        if groupByDirectory {
190|f958d9|            let grouped = Dictionary(grouping: processedResults) { $0.directory }
191|9c37af|            return grouped.sorted { $0.key < $1.key }.map { (key: $0.key, results: $0.value) }
192|b31999|        } else {

127|e66206|    /// Updates suggestions based on the current text and cursor.
128|2cbc84|    ///
129|d91771|    /// FEAT-046: extracts symbols from `text` and mixes them into the suggestion list.
130|785f23|    /// FEAT-047: adds a curated set of Swift stdlib completions.
131|6224c3|    func updateSuggestions(for text: String, cursorPosition: Int) {
132|4b5e56|        let safeCursor = max(0, min(cursorPosition, text.count))
133|97fb6b|        guard let context = completionContext(in: text, cursorPosition: safeCursor) else {
134|0efe98|            apply(items: [])
135|bef5d6|            return
136|5f3077|        }
137|adc83b|
138|c2e8b0|        let prefixLower = context.prefix.lowercased()
139|042f0f|        guard !prefixLower.isEmpty else {
140|bacf86|            // If user just typed a dot, show members even with empty prefix.
141|a46e04|            if context.isMemberCompletion, let base = context.memberBase {
142|c9f7f8|                let members = memberCandidates(forBase: base)
143|92798d|                let items = members.map { Suggestion(kind: .member, displayText: $0, score: 1000) }
144|0b887c|                apply(items: items)
145|f5a6eb|            } else {
146|4c73d4|                apply(items: [])
147|a7dc16|            }
148|bef5d6|            return
149|5f3077|        }
150|adc83b|
151|3e8861|        var candidates: [Suggestion] = []
152|adc83b|
153|67a42f|        // FEAT-046: current file symbols
154|f70c93|        let symbols = extractSymbols(from: text)
155|27a302|        candidates.append(contentsOf: symbols
156|488fb3|            .filter { $0.lowercased().hasPrefix(prefixLower) }
157|9de4dd|            .map { Suggestion(kind: .symbol, displayText: $0, score: 900) })
158|adc83b|
159|5f2431|        // Keywords
160|1a6e20|        candidates.append(contentsOf: keywords
161|488fb3|            .filter { $0.lowercased().hasPrefix(prefixLower) }
162|b40e7e|            .map { Suggestion(kind: .keyword, displayText: $0, score: 800) })
163|adc83b|
164|fcf131|        // FEAT-047: Swift stdlib (top level)
165|d76253|        candidates.append(contentsOf: stdlibTopLevel
166|488fb3|            .filter { $0.lowercased().hasPrefix(prefixLower) }
167|3cfc84|            .map { Suggestion(kind: .stdlib, displayText: $0, score: 700) })
168|adc83b|
169|07fafa|        // Member completions (very small heuristic-based set)
170|7f874f|        if context.isMemberCompletion, let base = context.memberBase {
171|68d0ac|            let members = memberCandidates(forBase: base)
172|a69811|            candidates.append(contentsOf: members
173|585680|                .filter { $0.lowercased().hasPrefix(prefixLower) }
174|73995e|                .map { Suggestion(kind: .member, displayText: $0, score: 1000) })
175|5f3077|        }
176|adc83b|
177|41630d|        // De-dupe + rank
178|673af4|        let merged = mergeAndSort(candidates)
179|678fc2|        apply(items: merged)
180|27e597|    }
181|adc83b|
182|530c2a|    func selectNext() {
183|1052ec|        guard showSuggestions else { return }
184|3185f4|        if selectedIndex < suggestions.count - 1 {
185|f3e28c|            selectedIndex += 1
186|5f3077|        }
187|27e597|    }
188|adc83b|
189|2b2ba9|    func selectPrevious() {
190|1052ec|        guard showSuggestions else { return }
191|1b2b81|        if selectedIndex > 0 {
192|ee2279|            selectedIndex -= 1
193|5f3077|        }
194|27e597|    }
195|adc83b|
196|3cfb82|    func getCurrentSuggestion() -> String? {
197|55f4f4|        guard showSuggestions, selectedIndex < suggestions.count else { return nil }
198|acf4b6|        return suggestions[selectedIndex]
199|27e597|    }

201|827001|    func hideSuggestions() {
202|338df5|        apply(items: [])
203|27e597|    }

205|b311f6|    /// Optional helper for inserting the currently-selected suggestion into the text.
206|68b7cb|    /// (Not wired by default; added as plumbing for FEAT-045 dropdown selection.)
207|85ca8d|    func commitCurrentSuggestion(into text: inout String, cursorPosition: inout Int) {
208|f15814|        guard let suggestion = suggestionItems[safe: selectedIndex], showSuggestions else { return }
209|4b5e56|        let safeCursor = max(0, min(cursorPosition, text.count))
210|2e795d|        guard let context = completionContext(in: text, cursorPosition: safeCursor) else { return }
211|adc83b|
212|9bab77|        let replacementRange = context.replacementRange
213|323d10|        text.replaceSubrange(replacementRange, with: suggestion.insertText)
214|adc83b|
215|8d1541|        // Move cursor to end of inserted text.
216|b73dac|        let newCursorOffset = text.distance(from: text.startIndex, to: replacementRange.lowerBound) + suggestion.insertText.count
217|68489c|        cursorPosition = min(newCursorOffset, text.count)
218|adc83b|
219|be2759|        hideSuggestions()
220|27e597|    }
221|adc83b|
222|07ac71|    // MARK: - Internals
223|adc83b|
224|7d7b95|    private struct CompletionContext {
225|0dee4e|        let prefix: String
226|b4787e|        let replacementRange: Range<String.Index>
227|56198f|        let isMemberCompletion: Bool
228|79772b|        let memberBase: String?
229|27e597|    }
230|adc83b|
231|f6601a|    private func completionContext(in text: String, cursorPosition: Int) -> CompletionContext? {
232|4c2df9|        guard !text.isEmpty else { return nil }
233|d6ed84|        
234|42915b|        // Safety check: ensure cursorPosition is within bounds
235|4b5e56|        let safeCursor = max(0, min(cursorPosition, text.count))
236|1fae78|        let cursorIndex = text.index(text.startIndex, offsetBy: safeCursor)
237|adc83b|
238|5aebf3|        // Find start of current identifier (letters/digits/_).
239|39f169|        var start = cursorIndex
240|26ebb3|        while start > text.startIndex {
241|c5c76e|            let prev = text.index(before: start)
242|9f8a31|            if isIdentifierChar(text[prev]) {
243|1929f8|                start = prev
244|f5a6eb|            } else {
245|74cfd8|                break
246|a7dc16|            }
247|5f3077|        }
248|adc83b|
249|bf292f|        let prefix = String(text[start..<cursorIndex])
250|adc83b|
251|824562|        // Member completion if immediately preceded by '.'
252|e374b4|        var isMember = false
253|e47c72|        var memberBase: String? = nil
254|adc83b|
255|0c2c38|        if start > text.startIndex {
256|2aa058|            let dotIndex = text.index(before: start)
257|88bd65|            if text[dotIndex] == "." {
258|ca8397|                isMember = true
259|adc83b|
260|6f6689|                // Parse identifier before '.'
261|91f615|                var baseEnd = dotIndex
262|521a36|                var baseStart = baseEnd
263|5fa357|                while baseStart > text.startIndex {
264|56e352|                    let prev = text.index(before: baseStart)
265|2a8ddd|                    if isIdentifierChar(text[prev]) {
266|fbabfa|                        baseStart = prev
267|540066|                    } else {
268|28a64b|                        break
269|c9717a|                    }
270|4e2d32|                }
271|f96abf|                let base = String(text[baseStart..<baseEnd])
272|ce472b|                if !base.isEmpty {
273|b9c992|                    memberBase = base
274|4e2d32|                }
275|a7dc16|            }
276|5f3077|        }
277|adc83b|
278|081616|        return CompletionContext(prefix: prefix,
279|c93ac4|                                 replacementRange: start..<cursorIndex,
280|a50c25|                                 isMemberCompletion: isMember,
281|ee9636|                                 memberBase: memberBase)
282|27e597|    }
283|adc83b|
284|818e4b|    private func isIdentifierChar(_ c: Character) -> Bool {
285|c233b9|        // Swift identifiers are more complex, but this is enough for basic autocomplete.
286|a164d4|        return c.isLetter || c.isNumber || c == "_"
287|27e597|    }
288|adc83b|
289|117bcf|    private func memberCandidates(forBase base: String) -> [String] {
290|cf1cb2|        // Basic heuristic: only match known stdlib types by exact name.
291|622249|        if let members = memberCompletions[base] { return members }
292|b72a10|        return []
293|27e597|    }
294|adc83b|
295|6ba6d8|    private func extractSymbols(from text: String) -> [String] {
296|1098cf|        // Very lightweight symbol extraction: looks for common declarations.
297|141450|        // Intentionally best-effort; keeps FEAT-046 self-contained.
298|f746d2|        var results = Set<String>()
299|adc83b|
300|f97d0d|        func addMatches(pattern: String) {
301|ca0afa|            guard let regex = try? NSRegularExpression(pattern: pattern, options: []) else { return }
302|6c811f|            let ns = text as NSString
303|b25f5b|            let range = NSRange(location: 0, length: ns.length)
304|d25847|            regex.enumerateMatches(in: text, options: [], range: range) { match, _, _ in
305|14f5aa|                guard let match, match.numberOfRanges >= 2 else { return }
306|345d9a|                let nameRange = match.range(at: 1)
307|de56e8|                guard nameRange.location != NSNotFound else { return }
308|8989a1|                let name = ns.substring(with: nameRange)
309|66b469|                if !name.isEmpty { results.insert(name) }
310|a7dc16|            }
311|5f3077|        }
312|adc83b|
313|a1c515|        // func Foo
314|cd4071|        addMatches(pattern: "\\bfunc\\s+([A-Za-z_][A-Za-z0-9_]*)")
315|5eaefb|        // class/struct/enum/protocol/typealias Foo
316|685691|        addMatches(pattern: "\\b(?:class|struct|enum|protocol|typealias)\\s+([A-Za-z_][A-Za-z0-9_]*)")
317|3764b8|        // let/var foo (captures first name before : = , )
318|bbf05c|        addMatches(pattern: "\\b(?:let|var)\\s+([A-Za-z_][A-Za-z0-9_]*)(?=\\s*[:=,])")
319|adc83b|
320|01a90c|        return results.sorted { $0.localizedCaseInsensitiveCompare($1) == .orderedAscending }

136|173529|        if context.coordinator.lastThemeId != currentThemeId {
137|0ae3b4|            context.coordinator.lastThemeId = currentThemeId

149|be78cc|        // Word wrap toggle still works

152|5f3077|        }
153|d6ed84|        
154|26756b|        // CRITICAL: Only call setState() when safe (not during active editing)
155|e2bb7b|        // Calling setState() during editing corrupts Runestone's lineManager
156|092fab|        // and causes crash at TextEditHelper.swift:27 (force unwrap on linePosition)
157|d6ed84|        
158|a43f62|        let isFileSwitching = context.coordinator.lastFilename != filename

177|3070d1|

180|3070d1|            
181|a6439c|            // Update line count
182|ebb427|            DispatchQueue.main.async {

184|a7dc16|            }
185|8bc7f3|        } else if textChanged && !context.coordinator.hasBeenEdited && !isActivelyEditing && !context.coordinator.isUpdatingFromTextView {
186|016671|            // Text changed externally (e.g., initial load, external modification)
187|51a126|            // Safe to update since user hasn't started editing yet
188|66a1a1|            if let language = getTreeSitterLanguage(for: filename) {

312|c746a1|        var count = 1
313|48817a|        var index = text.startIndex

319|5f3077|        }

50|6d9f0a|    /// Finds the matching bracket for the bracket at or near the given cursor position.
51|46e14e|    /// Returns nil if no bracket is found at the cursor position.
52|a86427|    func findMatchingBracket(in text: String, cursorPosition: Int) -> BracketPair? {
53|4c2df9|        guard !text.isEmpty else { return nil }
54|d6ed84|        
55|9df2e8|        let chars = Array(text)
56|7169cc|        let count = chars.count
57|d6ed84|        
58|eb0050|        // Clamp cursor position
59|112372|        let pos = max(0, min(cursorPosition, count))
60|d6ed84|        
61|404d74|        // Check character at cursor and before cursor
62|58bc54|        let positionsToCheck = [pos, pos - 1].filter { $0 >= 0 && $0 < count }
63|d6ed84|        
64|fd29be|        for checkPos in positionsToCheck {
65|a27369|            let char = chars[checkPos]
66|3070d1|            
67|e89ec3|            if let (bracketType, isOpen) = BracketType.from(char: char) {
68|3a7bbf|                if isOpen {
69|265e1e|                    // Search forward for closing bracket
70|817469|                    if let closeIndex = findClosingBracket(in: chars, from: checkPos, type: bracketType) {
71|0deeaf|                        return BracketPair(openIndex: checkPos, closeIndex: closeIndex, type: bracketType)
72|c9717a|                    }
73|fdd0e2|                } else {
74|e9cd75|                    // Search backward for opening bracket
75|b6a492|                    if let openIndex = findOpeningBracket(in: chars, from: checkPos, type: bracketType) {
76|7b17bb|                        return BracketPair(openIndex: openIndex, closeIndex: checkPos, type: bracketType)
77|c9717a|                    }
78|4e2d32|                }
79|a7dc16|            }
80|5f3077|        }
81|d6ed84|        
82|c2ae65|        return nil
83|27e597|    }

85|25e770|    /// Finds all bracket pairs in the given text.
86|81d973|    /// Useful for rainbow bracket coloring.
87|ff38bb|    func findAllBracketPairs(in text: String) -> [BracketPair] {
88|dcb8ea|        var pairs: [BracketPair] = []
89|3e3195|        var stacks: [BracketType: [Int]] = [:]
90|d6ed84|        
91|f022b0|        for type in BracketType.allCases {
92|54a3ff|            stacks[type] = []
93|5f3077|        }
94|d6ed84|        
95|9df2e8|        let chars = Array(text)
96|e79b86|        var inString = false
97|11024e|        var stringChar: Character = "\""
98|e550d2|        var escapeNext = false
99|d6ed84|        
100|f0ad7e|        for (index, char) in chars.enumerated() {
101|11cf75|            // Handle escape sequences
102|5c254a|            if escapeNext {
103|b7c801|                escapeNext = false
104|1df510|                continue
105|a7dc16|            }
106|3070d1|            
107|b316c9|            if char == "\\" {
108|78ee7a|                escapeNext = true
109|1df510|                continue
110|a7dc16|            }
111|3070d1|            
112|209ff5|            // Handle string literals
113|631cb5|            if char == "\"" || char == "'" {
114|9f8dba|                if !inString {
115|cce9f8|                    inString = true
116|fd9c87|                    stringChar = char
117|d26b9a|                } else if char == stringChar {
118|dffb64|                    inString = false
119|4e2d32|                }
120|1df510|                continue
121|a7dc16|            }
122|3070d1|            
123|801179|            // Skip brackets inside strings
124|28e059|            if inString { continue }
125|3070d1|            
126|ae2237|            // Check for brackets
127|e89ec3|            if let (bracketType, isOpen) = BracketType.from(char: char) {
128|3a7bbf|                if isOpen {
129|059a6a|                    stacks[bracketType]?.append(index)
130|fdd0e2|                } else {
131|a4ab35|                    if let openIndex = stacks[bracketType]?.popLast() {
132|25a92d|                        pairs.append(BracketPair(openIndex: openIndex, closeIndex: index, type: bracketType))
133|c9717a|                    }
134|4e2d32|                }
135|a7dc16|            }
136|5f3077|        }
137|d6ed84|        
138|4ca1cd|        return pairs.sorted { $0.openIndex < $1.openIndex }
139|27e597|    }

232|e79b86|        var inString = false
233|11024e|        var stringChar: Character = "\""
234|d6ed84|        
235|f6da67|        // For backward search, we need a simpler approach since escape sequences are tricky
236|fe2046|        // We'll do a basic scan that handles most common cases
237|267cd6|        for i in stride(from: startIndex - 1, through: 0, by: -1) {
238|8672ad|            let char = chars[i]
239|3070d1|

241|631cb5|            if char == "\"" || char == "'" {

243|d575e8|                if i > 0 && chars[i - 1] == "\\" {
244|f41bef|                    continue
245|4e2d32|                }
246|399b31|                inString = !inString
247|54e155|                stringChar = char
248|1df510|                continue
249|a7dc16|            }
250|3070d1|

252|3070d1|            
253|b67e2d|            if char == type.close {
254|4994cd|                depth += 1
255|d1d7f1|            } else if char == type.open {
256|ae2b9f|                depth -= 1
257|f13da5|                if depth == 0 {
258|125c3c|                    return i
259|4e2d32|                }
260|a7dc16|            }

208|7e9816|    public func search(in rootURL: URL,
209|058f9b|                       query: SearchQuery,
210|9bea17|                       fileURLs: [URL]? = nil) {

212|8ff3fb|        results = []

215|bdac63|        let trimmed = query.text.trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespacesAndNewlines)
216|658bd9|        guard !trimmed.isEmpty else {
217|18af28|            lastError = SearchError.emptyQuery.localizedDescription
218|bef5d6|            return
219|5f3077|        }
220|adc83b|
221|ebf179|        // update history immediately
222|4dd67e|        addToHistory(query)

224|7657bd|        cancelSearch()

227|2a4395|        let q = SearchQuery(text: trimmed,
228|827ce5|                            options: query.options,
229|407261|                            includeGlobs: query.includeGlobs,
230|9388a1|                            excludeGlobs: query.excludeGlobs)
231|adc83b|
232|9880df|        searchTask = Task.detached(priority: .userInitiated) { [weak self] in
233|bd7394|            guard let self else { return }
234|71cc09|            do {
235|030fd6|                let resolvedFiles = try self.resolveFiles(rootURL: rootURL, provided: fileURLs, query: q)
236|58e6ab|                let total = max(resolvedFiles.count, 1)
237|adc83b|
238|5b0c43|                var aggregated: [FileMatch] = []
239|5780de|                for (idx, url) in resolvedFiles.enumerated() {
240|257e20|                    try Task.checkCancellation()
241|bba096|                    if let match = try self.searchFile(url: url, rootURL: rootURL, query: q), !match.matches.isEmpty {
242|3c1aaf|                        aggregated.append(match)
243|c9717a|                    }
244|8080d2|                    let p = Double(idx + 1) / Double(total)
245|72e736|                    await MainActor.run {
246|a74df1|                        self.progress = p
247|c9717a|                    }
248|4e2d32|                }
249|adc83b|
250|41f488|                await MainActor.run {
251|3dcd82|                    self.results = aggregated

253|1050b1|                    self.progress = 1
254|4e2d32|                }
255|57e5c6|            } catch is CancellationError {
256|41f488|                await MainActor.run {
257|5abc40|                    self.isSearching = false
258|4e2d32|                }

260|41f488|                await MainActor.run {
261|f47429|                    self.lastError = error.localizedDescription
262|5abc40|                    self.isSearching = false
263|4e2d32|                }
264|a7dc16|            }
265|5f3077|        }
266|27e597|    }

311|e3e05b|    private func resolveFiles(rootURL: URL, provided: [URL]?, query: SearchQuery) throws -> [URL] {
312|657d5a|        let all: [URL]
313|070c1c|        if let provided {
314|cc4ad8|            all = provided
315|b31999|        } else {
316|eb4c22|            all = try enumerateFiles(rootURL: rootURL)
317|5f3077|        }
318|97b3ce|        return all.filter { url in

324|5f3077|        }
325|27e597|    }

327|23fd14|    private func enumerateFiles(rootURL: URL) throws -> [URL] {

329|613364|        guard let enumerator = fm.enumerator(at: rootURL,

334|5f3077|        }

337|3377e0|        for case let url as URL in enumerator {

342|a7dc16|            }
343|5f3077|        }
344|a10f36|        return urls
345|27e597|    }

127|e66206|    /// Updates suggestions based on the current text and cursor.
128|2cbc84|    ///
129|d91771|    /// FEAT-046: extracts symbols from `text` and mixes them into the suggestion list.
130|785f23|    /// FEAT-047: adds a curated set of Swift stdlib completions.
131|6224c3|    func updateSuggestions(for text: String, cursorPosition: Int) {
132|4b5e56|        let safeCursor = max(0, min(cursorPosition, text.count))
133|97fb6b|        guard let context = completionContext(in: text, cursorPosition: safeCursor) else {

135|bef5d6|            return
136|5f3077|        }
137|adc83b|
138|c2e8b0|        let prefixLower = context.prefix.lowercased()

149|5f3077|        }
150|adc83b|

152|adc83b|

154|f70c93|        let symbols = extractSymbols(from: text)

165|d76253|        candidates.append(contentsOf: stdlibTopLevel

167|3cfc84|            .map { Suggestion(kind: .stdlib, displayText: $0, score: 700) })

171|68d0ac|            let members = memberCandidates(forBase: base)
172|a69811|            candidates.append(contentsOf: members

175|5f3077|        }
176|adc83b|

178|673af4|        let merged = mergeAndSort(candidates)
179|678fc2|        apply(items: merged)
180|27e597|    }

254|adc83b|

786|eacbbe|        func applySyntaxHighlighting(to textView: UITextView) {
787|a71899|            // Guard against reentrancy - this can happen if attributedText assignment
788|eea832|            // triggers delegate callbacks that call this method again
789|8ebaf1|            guard !isApplyingHighlighting else { return }
790|cfeb02|            isApplyingHighlighting = true
791|819888|            defer { isApplyingHighlighting = false }
792|3070d1|            
793|6035ba|            let theme = ThemeManager.shared.currentTheme
794|66d0d9|            lastThemeId = theme.id
795|adc83b|
796|e30342|            let highlighter = VSCodeSyntaxHighlighter(theme: theme, fontSize: parent.editorCore.editorFontSize)
797|4ba13c|            let attributedText = highlighter.highlight(textView.text, filename: parent.filename)
798|adc83b|
799|e844dd|            let selectedRange = textView.selectedRange
800|adc83b|
801|b096af|            // NOTE: We intentionally do NOT manipulate undoManager.disableUndoRegistration/enableUndoRegistration
802|bf1d61|            // here. UITextView's internal undo manager state machine is fragile and can crash with
803|b755b7|            // "enableUndoRegistration may only be invoked with matching call to disableUndoRegistration"
804|dd5c2c|            // when attributedText assignment triggers internal undo callbacks.
805|75d880|            // 
806|ff6bb4|            // Instead, we let the system handle undo naturally. The trade-off is that syntax highlighting
807|92400f|            // changes might add noise to the undo stack, but this is preferable to crashing.
808|3070d1|            
809|82cb50|            textView.attributedText = attributedText
810|335b1a|            textView.selectedRange = selectedRange
811|adc83b|
812|cc87a2|            // Set typing attributes so newly typed characters have correct base styling
813|246348|            // This prevents flicker during the debounce period before full highlighting runs
814|810685|            let fontSize = parent.editorCore.editorFontSize
815|426131|            textView.typingAttributes = [
816|69640c|                .font: UIFont.monospacedSystemFont(ofSize: fontSize, weight: .regular),
817|247992|                .foregroundColor: UIColor(theme.editorForeground)
818|324820|            ]
819|adc83b|
820|b7d37f|            // FEAT-044: restore matching bracket highlight after re-attributing text
821|a9be52|            updateMatchingBracketHighlight(textView)
822|5f3077|        }

883|b56d26|        func handleToggleComment(in textView: UITextView) {
884|8a6136|            guard let selectedRange = textView.selectedTextRange else { return }
885|b3d375|            let text = textView.text ?? ""
886|3070d1|            
887|498552|            // Get the current line range
888|59308e|            if let lineRange = textView.tokenizer.rangeEnclosingPosition(selectedRange.start, with: .paragraph, inDirection: UITextDirection(rawValue: 1)) {
889|082b9d|                let location = textView.offset(from: textView.beginningOfDocument, to: lineRange.start)
890|b79460|                let length = textView.offset(from: lineRange.start, to: lineRange.end)
891|3a65b5|                let nsRange = NSRange(location: location, length: length)
892|216278|                
893|cf8d27|                if nsRange.location + nsRange.length <= (text as NSString).length {
894|01a1cd|                    let lineText = (text as NSString).substring(with: nsRange)
895|c7935c|                    let trimmed = lineText.trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespaces)
896|dd2193|                    
897|63b596|                    // Check if line starts with a comment
898|e2244f|                    let isCommented = trimmed.hasPrefix("//") || trimmed.hasPrefix("#") || trimmed.hasPrefix("/*")
899|dd2193|                    
900|8d6cd7|                    // Toggle comment
901|1073f5|                    var newLineText: String
902|f89255|                    if isCommented {

904|742191|                        newLineText = lineText.replacingOccurrences(of: "//", with: "").replacingOccurrences(of: "#", with: "", options: .anchored)
905|540066|                    } else {

907|ea84d0|                        newLineText = "//" + lineText
908|c9717a|                    }
909|dd2193|                    
910|2fe9fd|                    // Replace the line

912|dddbeb|                    textStorage.replaceCharacters(in: nsRange, with: newLineText)
